  3: "Human Characteristics"
  3: "Human Culture"
  3: "Human History"
  3: "Back"
  3: "CHAT_CHANNEL_JOURNAL"
  3: "Humans are the dominant sentient species in the Kingdom of Morella. Smaller than orcs and shorter than elves, they are most physically distinguished by their agility."
  3: "Magical affinity is rare among humans. Less than 1 in 1000 possess the gift, and most of those that do are quickly adopted by one of the major temples."
  3: "Humans in Morella are organized in a traditional monarchy; the seat of power is with the king in the capital city, who carries out his will through two dozen local lords."
  3: "Even with the one Kingdom, human culture is divided into many subcultures and groups, from the decadent nobles of Whitetower to the seafaring rogues of Parnassus. If there\'s one consistent trait to humanity, it might be their inconsistency."
  3: "Two thousand years ago, during the era of the elven empire, humans were largely a servant caste to the elves, acting as laborers and farmers for the many elven houses."
  3: "However, after the elven civilization fell in the Great War, humans flourished. They took over many of the elven cities and manors, and quickly created an impressive civilization of their own."
  3: "For about 500 years, Morella was divided into two dozen fiefdoms, constantly at war. But this period of darkness and chaos ended when the  Lords of Whitetower triumphed, conquering the territories one by one to create a unified dynasty."
  3: "Since then, the Valleros Dynasty from Whitetower has ruled over the humans of Morella, barring the occasional civil war and peasant uprising."
  3: "King Arlan Valleros VII currently sits on the throne. Known as the Gentle King, Arlan has reigned over a period of great peace and prosperity. He has two sons: Baldur and Aerin."
  3: "Read about..."
  3: "Orc Characteristics"
  3: "Orc Culture"
  3: "Orc History"
  3: "Back"
  3: "Orcs are the largest and strongest of the sentient species of Morella. The average orc stands six and a half feet tall, and has the muscle mass of the most well-built of humans."
  3: "Orcs possess tremendous physical strength. Their strongest can bend steel with their bare hands and withstand extreme heat and cold."
  3: "Female orcs are stronger than males, which, given the emphasis on physical prowess in their culture, means most orcish fleets are matriarchal."
  3: "Magic use in orcs is extremely rare. Less than 1 in 10000 orcs are capable of magic."
  3: "Orcs are a nomadic species. \'We Lay No Roots\' is a foundational principle of orcish culture, and one held deeply by all Clans. Travel, adventure, and the thrill of conquest... these are the values orcs hold dear."
  3: "Orcs are a seafaring race. They are divided into twelve fleets, each made up of several hundred members."
  3: "Orcs do not worship Gods like the humans or elves. Rather, they worship elements of nature: the Ocean, the Sky, the Stars and the Moon."
  3: "According to orcish legend, they hail from a land far to the east, a continent known as K\'ell Dhana... \'The World That Was\'. There, they once had a massive civilization, an empire that puts the Kingdom of Morella to shame."
  3: "After K\'ell Dhana was destroyed in a great volcanic eruption, the orcs who survived took to the seas and vowed to always keep moving, never settle, and never grow beyond their means."
  3: "In the past, the twelve orcish fleets acted independently, even in conflict. But ten years ago, they were united under the leadership of Ventra Tal Kaelen, who formed an alliance and established a capital, the floating city of Flotilla."
  3: "Read about..."
  3: "Elf Characteristics"
  3: "Elf Culture"
  3: "Elf History"
  3: "Back"
  3: "Elves are taller than humans, standing an average of just over six feet tall. Elves also possess incredible senses, capable of seeing the tiniest drop of dew on a blade of grass or hearing a whisper two rooms away."
  3: "Elves are also long-lived; the average elf lives to three hundred years old! They reach maturity at about 50, and then maintain that appearance until their oldest years."
  3: "All elves possess some degree of magical affinity. From an early age, elven children are sorted into magical schools which train their talents, from Green Naturalists to Purple Illusionists to Black Battlemages."
  3: "After the Great War, there are only five hundred or so elves left alive. Outside of a handful of exiles and outcasts, they all live in the city of Undermount in the north."
  3: "An incredibly complex hierarchy exists among all the elven houses, with an ever-shifting ladder of rank and wealth. Social competition is a cornerstone of elven society, and many elves spend their whole lives trying to advance the standing of their house."
  3: "The elven empire was once the greatest in the world, a glorious civilization spanning Morella and beyond. For a thousand years, elves lived in peace and prosperity. Their society was built on magic, and magic elevated them to greatness."
  3: "But their magic was also their downfall. Their pursuit of ever-greater power opened a doorway to the Realm of Shadow, and the dark powers therein. The Great War began... and a hundred years later, the elves were all but wiped out."
  3: "The only survivors were those sheltered in the great sanctuary of Undermount. For nearly four centuries, they sealed themselves away, refusing all contact with the outside world."
  3: "Now, elves have, somewhat reluctantly, reopened their gates. Undermount exists in an odd political space: while it exists within the boundaries of Morella, the humans have no jurisdiction over it, and it operates as an autonomous city-state."
  3: "Orcs, elves and humans are the primary sentient species on Morella, but there are a few others of note."
  3: "The amphibious grobtars live in the ocean depths. Little is known of their culture save unreliable accounts from captured sailors, but they are feared for their vicious, merciless attacks on traveling ships."
  3: "The vhampyr live in the crypts of the ruined city of Necropolis. Some believe the bloodsucking immortals to be cursed elves; others think they\'re not living at all, but ghosts made flesh. Given that no traveller has ever made it out of their city alive, perhaps we\'ll never know."
  3: "There are many others as well: the mermen of the Shimmering Isles, the molepeople of the Red Desert, the legendary birdmen of the north. Some even believe the drakna, horrifying as they are, are sentient and have a secret society in the Deadwood!"
